<P class="p28 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft13">Lagen ska till√§mpas i fr√•ga om</SPAN></P>
<P class="p29 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">k√§llskatter, p√• belopp som betalas eller tillgodof√∂rs den 1 januari det √•r som f√∂ljer n√§rmast efter den dag d√• lagen tr√§der i kraft eller senare, och</SPAN></P>
<P class="p30 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">andra skatter p√• inkomst och p√• f√∂rm√∂genhet, p√• skatt som tas ut f√∂r beskattnings√•r som b√∂rjar den 1 januari det √•r som f√∂ljer n√§rmast efter den dag d√• lagen tr√§der i kraft eller senare.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p31 ft3">4</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_5">


<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p12 ft3"><SPAN class="ft4">Bilaga </SPAN>Prop. 2013/14:149</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p32 ft12">Avtal mellan Sveriges regering och Georgiens regering f√∂r undvikande av dubbelbeskattning och f√∂rhindrande av skatteflykt betr√§ffande skatter p√• inkomst och p√• f√∂rm√∂genhet</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p32 ft12">Convention between the Government of Sweden and the Government of Georgia for the avoidance of double taxation and the prevention of fiscal evasion with respect to taxes on income and on capital</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p33 ft3">Sveriges regering och Georgiens regering, som √∂nskar ing√• ett avtal f√∂r undvikande av dubbelbeskattning och f√∂rhindrande av skatteflykt betr√§ffande skatter p√• inkomst och p√• f√∂rm√∂genhet, har kommit √∂verens om f√∂ljande:</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p33 ft3">The Government of Sweden and the Government of Georgia, desiring to conclude a Convention for the avoidance of double taxation and the prevention of fiscal evasion with respect to taxes on income and on capital, have agreed as follows:</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t4">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr3 td17"><SPAN class="p3 ft11">Artikel 1</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr3 td18"><SPAN class="p3 ft11">Article 1</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr8 td17"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Personer p√• vilka avtalet till√§mpas</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr8 td18"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Persons covered</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_5">
<DIV id="id_5_1">
<P class="p34 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Detta avtal till√§mpas p√• personer som har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat eller i b√•da avtalsslutande staterna.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p34 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">Inkomst som f√∂rv√§rvas av eller genom en person vars inkomst enligt lagstiftningen i endera avtalsslutande staten √§r f√∂rem√•l f√∂r del√§garbeskattning, ska anses f√∂rv√§rvad av en person med hemvist i en av staterna till den del som inkomsten, enligt skattelagstiftningen i denna stat, behandlas som inkomst hos en person med hemvist</SPAN></P>
<P class="p35 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">i</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">staten i fr√•ga.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_5_2">
<P class="p33 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft7">This Convention shall apply to persons who are residents of one or both of the Contracting States.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p36 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft17">In the case of an item of income derived by or through a person that is fiscally transparent under the laws of either Contracting State, such item shall be considered to be derived by a resident of a State to the extent that the item is treated for the purposes of the taxation law of such State as the income of a resident.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>

<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p12 ft4">Allm√§nna definitioner</P>
<P class="p48 ft5">1. Om inte sammanhanget f√∂ranleder annat, har vid till√§mpningen av detta avtal f√∂ljande uttryck nedan angiven betydelse:</P>
<P class="p34 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft19">‚ÄùGeorgien‚Äù avser det territorium s√•som detta definieras i georgisk lagstiftning, innefattande det landomr√•de, dess underlag och luftrummet √∂ver detta omr√•de, samt inre vatten och territorialhav, havsbottnen, dess underlag och luftrummet √∂ver dessa omr√•den, inom vilket Georgien ut√∂var suver√§nitet, och den angr√§nsande zonen, den exklusiva ekonomiska zonen och kontinentalsockeln som gr√§nsar till territorialhavet, inom vilka Georgien ut√∂var suver√§na r√§ttigheter eller jurisdiktion i √∂verensst√§mmelse med folkr√§ttens regler,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p49 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">‚ÄùSverige‚Äù avser Konungariket Sverige och, n√§r uttrycket anv√§nds i geografisk betydelse, innefattar Sveriges territorium, Sveriges territorialhav och andra havsomr√•den √∂ver vilka Sverige i √∂verensst√§mmelse med folkr√§ttens regler ut√∂var suver√§na r√§ttigheter eller jurisdiktion,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p49 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft21">‚Äùen avtalsslutande stat‚Äù och ‚Äùden andra avtalsslutande staten‚Äù avser Georgien eller Sverige, beroende p√• sammanhanget,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p34 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft22">‚Äùperson‚Äù inbegriper fysisk person, bolag och annan sammanslutning,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p50 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft23">‚Äùbolag‚Äù avser juridisk person eller annan som vid beskattningen behandlas s√•som juridisk person,</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p12 ft4">General definitions</P>
<P class="p52 ft9">1. For the purposes of this Convention, unless the context otherwise requires:</P>
<P class="p53 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">the term ‚ÄúGeorgia‚Äù means the territory defined by Georgian legislation, including land territory, its subsoil and the air space above it, internal waters and territorial sea, the sea bed, its </SPAN><NOBR>sub-soil</NOBR> and the air space above them, in respect of which Georgia exercises sovereignty, as well as the contiguous zone, the exclusive economic zone and continental shelf adjacent to its territorial sea, in respect of which Georgia may exercise its sovereign rights and/or jurisdiction in accordance with the international law;</P>
<P class="p54 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">the term ‚ÄúSweden‚Äù means the Kingdom of Sweden and, when used in a geographical sense, includes the national territory, the territorial sea of Sweden as well as other maritime areas over which Sweden in accordance with international law exercises sovereign rights or jurisdiction;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p55 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft26">the terms ‚Äúa Contracting State‚Äù and ‚Äúthe other Contracting State‚Äù mean Georgia or Sweden, as the context requires;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p56 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">the term ‚Äúperson‚Äù includes an individual, a company and any other body of persons;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p56 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft27">the term ‚Äúcompany‚Äù means any body corporate or any entity that is treated as a body corporate for tax purposes;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p56 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft23">the term ‚Äúenterprise‚Äù applies to the carrying on of any business;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p12 ft11">Artikel 4</P>
<P class="p62 ft4">Hemvist</P>
<P class="p48 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft19">Vid till√§mpningen av detta avtal avser uttrycket ‚Äùperson med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat‚Äù person som enligt lagstiftningen i denna stat √§r skattskyldig d√§r p√• grund av domicil, bos√§ttning, plats f√∂r f√∂retagsledning eller annan liknande omst√§ndighet och innefattar ocks√• denna stat, dess offentligr√§ttsliga organ eller institutioner, politiska underavdelningar eller lokala myndigheter. Detta uttryck inbegriper emellertid inte person som √§r skattskyldig i denna stat endast f√∂r inkomst fr√•n k√§lla i denna stat eller f√∂r f√∂rm√∂genhet bel√§gen d√§r.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p63 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">D√• p√• grund av best√§mmelserna i punkt 1 fysisk person har hemvist i b√•da avtalsslutande staterna, best√§ms hans hemvist p√• f√∂ljande s√§tt:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p64 ft3">a) han anses ha hemvist endast i den stat d√§r han har en bostad som stadigvarande st√•r till hans f√∂rfogande. Om han har en s√•dan bostad i b√•da staterna, anses han ha hemvist endast i den stat med vilken hans personliga och ekonomiska f√∂rbindelser √§r starkast (centrum f√∂r levnadsintressena),</P>
<P class="p49 ft3">b) om det inte kan avg√∂ras i vilken stat han har centrum f√∂r sina levnadsintressen eller om han inte i n√•gondera staten har en bostad som stadigvarande st√•r till hans f√∂rfogande, anses han ha hemvist endast i den stat d√§r han stadigvarande vistas,</P>
<P class="p64 ft3">c) om han stadigvarande vistas i b√•da staterna eller om han inte vistas stadigvarande i n√•gon av dem, anses han ha hemvist endast i den stat d√§r han √§r medborgare,</P>
<P class="p65 ft5">d) om han √§r medborgare i b√•da staterna eller om han inte √§r medborgare i n√•gon av dem, ska de</P>

	<TD class="tr13 td52"><SPAN class="p3 ft11">Article 4</SPAN> </TD>

<P class="p66 ft4">Resident</P>
<P class="p67 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">For the purposes of this Convention, the term ‚Äúresident of a Contracting State‚Äù means any person who, under the laws of that State, is liable to tax therein by reason of his domicile, residence, place of management or any other criterion of a similar nature, and also includes that State and any governmental body or agency, political subdivision or local authority thereof. This term, however, does not include any person who is liable to tax in that State in respect only of income from sources in that State or capital situated therein.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p68 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">Where by reason of the provisions of paragraph 1 an individual is a resident of both Contracting States, then his status shall be determined as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p69 ft3">a) he shall be deemed to be a resident only of the State in which he has a permanent home available to him; if he has a permanent home available to him in both States, he shall be deemed to be a resident only of the State with which his personal and economic relations are closer (centre of vital interests);</P>
<P class="p70 ft3">b) if the State in which he has his centre of vital interests cannot be determined, or if he has not a permanent home available to him in either State, he shall be deemed to be a resident only of the State in which he has an habitual abode;</P>
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">if he has an habitual abode in both States or in neither of them, he shall be deemed to be a resident only of the State of which he is a national;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p71 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">if he is a national of both</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t8">

<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p93 ft5">Prop. 2013/14:149 denna stadigvarande plats f√∂r aff√§rsverksamhet till fast driftst√§lle enligt best√§mmelserna i n√§mnda punkt.</P>
<P class="p94 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft17">F√∂retag anses inte ha fast driftst√§lle i en avtalsslutande stat endast p√• den grund att f√∂retaget bedriver aff√§rsverksamhet i denna stat genom f√∂rmedling av m√§klare, kommission√§r eller annan oberoende representant, under f√∂ruts√§ttning att s√•dan person d√§rvid bedriver sin sedvanliga aff√§rsverksamhet.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p95 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">7.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft17">Den omst√§ndigheten att ett bolag med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat kontrollerar eller kontrolleras av ett bolag med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten eller ett bolag som bedriver aff√§rsverksamhet i denna andra stat (antingen fr√•n fast driftst√§lle eller p√• annat s√§tt) medf√∂r inte i sig att n√•gotdera bolaget utg√∂r fast driftst√§lle f√∂r det andra.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p32 ft3">exercised through a fixed place of business, would not make this fixed place of business a permanent establishment under the provisions of that paragraph.</P>
<P class="p96 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft17">An enterprise shall not be deemed to have a permanent establishment in a Contracting State merely because it carries on business in that State through a broker, general commission agent or any other agent of an independent status, provided that such persons are acting in the ordinary course of their business.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p97 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">7.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">The fact that a company which is a resident of a Contracting State controls or is controlled by a company which is a resident of the other Contracting State, or which carries on business in that other State (whether through a permanent establishment or otherwise), shall not of itself constitute either company a permanent establishment of the other.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>

<P class="p12 ft11">Article 6</P>
<P class="p62 ft4">Income from immovable property</P>
<P class="p103 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">Income derived by a resident of a Contracting State from immovable property (including income from agriculture or forestry) situated in the other Contracting State may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p104 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft17">The term ‚Äúimmovable property‚Äù shall have the meaning which it has under the law of the Contracting State in which the property in question is situated. The term shall in any case include property accessory to immovable property, livestock and equipment used in agriculture and forestry, rights to which the provisions of general law respecting landed property apply, buildings, usufruct of immovable property and rights</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_13">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p32 ft5">ers√§ttningar f√∂r nyttjandet av eller r√§tten att nyttja mineralf√∂rekomst, k√§lla eller annan naturtillg√•ng. Skepp, b√•tar och luftfartyg anses inte vara fast egendom.</P>
<P class="p105 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft30">Best√§mmelserna i punkt 1 till√§mpas p√• inkomst som f√∂rv√§rvas genom omedelbart brukande, genom uthyrning eller annan anv√§ndning av fast egendom.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p106 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Best√§mmelserna i punkterna 1 och 3 till√§mpas √§ven p√• inkomst av fast egendom som tillh√∂r f√∂retag.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p12 ft5">to variable or fixed payments as Prop. 2013/14:149 consideration for the working of,</P>
<P class="p107 ft3">or the right to work, mineral deposits, sources and other natural resources; ships, boats and aircraft shall not be regarded as immovable property.</P>
<P class="p108 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The provisions of paragraph 1 shall apply to income derived from the direct use, letting, or use in any other form of immovable property.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p109 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft31">The provisions of paragraphs 1 and 3 shall also apply to the income from immovable property of an enterprise.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p12 ft11">Artikel 7</P>
<P class="p37 ft4">Inkomst av r√∂relse</P>
<P class="p110 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">Inkomst av r√∂relse, som f√∂retag i en avtalsslutande stat f√∂rv√§rvar, beskattas endast i denna stat, s√•vida inte f√∂retaget bedriver r√∂relse i den andra avtalsslutande staten fr√•n d√§r bel√§get fast driftst√§lle. Om f√∂retaget bedriver r√∂relse p√• nyss angivet s√§tt, f√•r f√∂retagets inkomst beskattas i den andra staten, men endast s√• stor del d√§rav som √§r h√§nf√∂rlig till det fasta driftst√§llet.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p63 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Om f√∂retag i en avtalsslutande stat bedriver r√∂relse i den andra avtalsslutande staten fr√•n d√§r bel√§get fast driftst√§lle h√§nf√∂rs, om inte best√§mmelserna i punkt 3 f√∂ranleder annat, i vardera avtalsslutande staten till det fasta driftst√§llet den inkomst som det kan antas att driftst√§llet skulle ha f√∂rv√§rvat, om det varit ett frist√•ende f√∂retag som bedrivit verksamhet av samma eller liknande slag under samma eller liknande villkor och sj√§lvst√§ndigt avslutat aff√§rer med det f√∂retag till vilket driftst√§llet h√∂r.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p111 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">Vid best√§mmande av fast drift-</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p12 ft11">Article 7</P>
<P class="p37 ft4">Business profits</P>
<P class="p112 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The profits of an enterprise of a Contracting State shall be taxable only in that State unless the enterprise carries on business in the other Contracting State through a permanent establishment situated therein. If the enterprise carries on business as aforesaid, the profits of the enterprise may be taxed in the other State but only so much of them as is attributable to that permanent establishment.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p113 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft27">Subject to the provisions of paragraph 3, where an enterprise of a Contracting State carries on business in the other Contracting State through a permanent establishment situated therein, there shall in each Contracting State be attributed to that permanent establishment the profits which it might be expected to make if it were a distinct and separate enterprise engaged in the same or similar activities under the same or similar conditions and dealing wholly independently with the enterprise of which it is a permanent establishment.</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t12">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr13 td125"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">3. In determining the profits of a</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr13 td126"><SPAN class="p15 ft3">13</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>

<P class="p93 ft3">Prop. 2013/14:149 st√§lles inkomst medges avdrag f√∂r utgifter som uppkommit f√∂r det fasta driftst√§llets verksamhet, h√§runder inbegripna utgifter f√∂r f√∂retagets ledning och allm√§nna f√∂rvaltning, oavsett om utgifterna uppkommit i den stat d√§r det fasta driftst√§llet √§r bel√§get eller annorst√§des.</P>
<P class="p114 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">Inkomst h√§nf√∂rs inte till fast driftst√§lle endast av den anledningen att varor ink√∂ps genom det fasta driftst√§llets f√∂rsorg f√∂r f√∂retaget.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p115 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft17">Vid till√§mpningen av f√∂reg√•ende punkter best√§ms inkomst som √§r h√§nf√∂rlig till det fasta driftst√§llet genom samma f√∂rfarande √•r fr√•n √•r, s√•vida inte goda och tillr√§ckliga sk√§l f√∂ranleder annat.</SPAN></P>

</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p32 ft3">permanent establishment, there shall be allowed as deductions expenses which are incurred for the purposes of the business of the permanent establishment, including executive and general administrative expenses so incurred, whether in the State in which the permanent establishment is situated or elsewhere.</P>
<P class="p106 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">No profits shall be attributed to a permanent establishment by reason of the mere purchase by that permanent establishment of goods or merchandise for the enterprise.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p117 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">For the purposes of the preceding paragraphs, the profits to be attributed to the permanent establishment shall be determined by the same method year by year unless there is good and sufficient reason to the contrary.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p118 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft7">Where profits include items of income which are dealt with separately in other Articles of this Convention, then the provisions of those Articles shall not be affected by the provisions of this Article.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p12 ft11">Article 8</P>
<P class="p37 ft4">Shipping and air transport</P>
<P class="p120 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">Profits of an enterprise of a Contracting State from the operation of ships or aircraft in international traffic shall be taxable only in that State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p121 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">With respect to profits derived by the air transport consortium Scandinavian Airlines System (SAS) the provisions of paragraph 1 shall apply only to such part of the profits as corresponds to the participation held in that consortium by SAS Sverige AB, the Swedish partner of SAS.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p122 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The provisions of paragraph 1 shall also apply to profits from the participation in a pool, a joint business or an international</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_15">


<DIV>
<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p12 ft3">internationell driftsorganisation.</P>
<P class="p62 ft11">Artikel 9</P>
<P class="p37 ft4">F√∂retag med intressegemenskap</P>
<P class="p123 ft3">1. I fall d√•</P>

<P class="p127 ft11">Artikel 10</P>
<P class="p128 ft4">Utdelning</P>
<P class="p129 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft13">Utdelning fr√•n bolag med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat till person med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten f√•r beskattas i denna andra stat.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p130 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">Utdelningen f√•r emellertid beskattas √§ven i den avtalsslutande stat d√§r bolaget som betalar utdelningen har hemvist, enligt lagstiftningen i denna stat, men om den som har r√§tt till utdelningen har hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten f√•r skatten inte √∂verstiga:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p131 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft30">0 procent av utdelningens bruttobelopp om den som har r√§tt till utdelningen √§r ett bolag (med undantag f√∂r handelsbolag) som innehar minst 10 procent av det utdelande bolagets kapital eller r√∂stetal,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p132 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft21">10 procent av utdelningens bruttobelopp i √∂vriga fall.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p133 ft5">Denna punkt ber√∂r inte bolagets beskattning f√∂r den vinst av vilken utdelningen betalas.</P>
<P class="p134 ft3">3. Med uttrycket ‚Äùutdelning‚Äù f√∂rst√•s i denna artikel inkomst av aktier eller andra r√§ttigheter, som inte √§r fordringar, med r√§tt till andel i vinst, samt inkomst av andra r√§ttigheter i bolag som enligt lagstiftningen i den stat d√§r det utdelande bolaget har hemvist vid beskattningen behandlas p√• samma s√§tt som inkomst av aktier.</P>

<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p12 ft11">Article 10</P>
<P class="p62 ft4">Dividends</P>
<P class="p120 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Dividends paid by a company which is a resident of a Contracting State to a resident of the other Contracting State may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p137 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">However, such dividends may also be taxed in the Contracting State of which the company paying the dividends is a resident and according to the laws of that State, but if the beneficial owner of the dividends is a resident of the other Contracting State, the tax so charged shall not exceed:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p138 ft3">a) 0 per cent of the gross amount of the dividends if the beneficial owner is a company (other than a partnership) which holds at least 10 per cent of the capital or the voting power of the company paying the dividends;</P>
<P class="p139 ft5">b) 10 per cent of the gross amount of the dividends in all other cases.</P>
<P class="p140 ft3">This paragraph shall not affect the taxation of the company in respect of the profits out of which the dividends are paid.</P>
<P class="p140 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The term ‚Äúdividends‚Äù as used in this Article means income from shares or other rights, not being </SPAN><NOBR>debt-claims,</NOBR> participating in profits, as well as income from other corporate rights which is subjected to the same taxation treatment as income from shares by the laws of the State of which the company making the distribution is a resident.</P>
<P class="p141 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">The provisions of paragraphs</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_17">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p32 ft3">och 2 till√§mpas inte, om den som har r√§tt till utdelningen har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat och bedriver r√∂relse i den andra avtalsslutande staten, d√§r bolaget som betalar utdelningen har hemvist, fr√•n d√§r bel√§get fast driftst√§lle, samt den andel p√• grund av vilken utdelningen betalas √§ger verkligt samband med det fasta driftst√§llet. I s√•dant fall till√§mpas best√§mmelserna i artikel 7.</P>
<P class="p142 ft3">5. Om bolag med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat f√∂rv√§rvar inkomst fr√•n den andra avtalsslutande staten, f√•r denna andra stat inte beskatta utdelning som bolaget betalar, utom i den m√•n utdelningen betalas till person med hemvist i denna andra stat eller i den m√•n den andel p√• grund av vilken utdelningen betalas √§ger verkligt samband med fast driftst√§lle i denna andra stat, och ej heller p√• bolagets icke utdelade vinst ta ut en skatt som utg√•r p√• bolagets icke utdelade vinst, √§ven om utdelningen eller den icke utdelade vinsten helt eller delvis utg√∂rs av inkomst som uppkommit i denna andra stat.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p12 ft5">1 and 2 shall not apply if the Prop. 2013/14:149 beneficial owner of the dividends,</P>
<P class="p107 ft3">being a resident of a Contracting State, carries on business in the other Contracting State of which the company paying the dividends is a resident through a permanent establishment situated therein and the holding in respect of which the dividends are paid is effectively connected with such permanent establishment. In such case the provisions of Article 7 shall apply.</P>
<P class="p143 ft3">5. Where a company which is a resident of a Contracting State derives profits or income from the other Contracting State, that other State may not impose any tax on the dividends paid by the company, except insofar as such dividends are paid to a resident of that other State or insofar as the holding in respect of which the dividends are paid is effectively connected with a permanent establishment situated in that other State, nor subject the company‚Äôs undistributed profits to a tax on the company‚Äôs undistributed profits, even if the dividends paid or the undistributed profits consist wholly or partly of profits or income arising in such other State.</P>
</DIV>

<DIV>
<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p32 ft3">i denna artikel varje slags betalning som tas emot s√•som ers√§ttning f√∂r nyttjandet av eller f√∂r r√§tten att nyttja upphovsr√§tt till litter√§rt, konstn√§rligt eller vetenskapligt verk, h√§ri inbegripet biograffilm och filmer eller band f√∂r radio- eller televisionsuts√§ndning, patent, varum√§rke, m√∂nster eller modell, ritning, hemligt recept eller hemlig tillverkningsmetod, eller f√∂r upplysning om erfarenhetsr√∂n av industriell, kommersiell eller vetenskaplig natur.</P>
<P class="p146 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft30">Best√§mmelserna i punkt 1 till√§mpas inte om den som har r√§tt till royaltyn har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat och bedriver r√∂relse i den andra avtalsslutande staten, fr√•n vilken royaltyn h√§rr√∂r, fr√•n d√§r bel√§get fast driftst√§lle, samt den r√§ttighet eller egendom i fr√•ga om vilken royaltyn betalas √§ger verkligt samband med det fasta driftst√§llet. I s√•dant fall till√§mpas best√§mmelserna i artikel 7.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p147 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft30">D√• p√• grund av s√§rskilda f√∂rbindelser mellan utbetalaren och den som har r√§tt till royaltyn eller mellan dem b√•da och annan person royaltybeloppet, med h√§nsyn till det nyttjande, den r√§ttighet eller den upplysning f√∂r vilken royaltyn betalas, √∂verstiger det belopp som skulle ha avtalats mellan utbetalaren och den som har r√§tt till royaltyn om s√•dana f√∂rbindelser inte f√∂relegat, till√§mpas best√§mmelserna i denna artikel endast p√• sistn√§mnda belopp. I s√•dant fall beskattas √∂verskjutande belopp enligt lagstiftningen i vardera avtalsslutande staten med iakttagande av √∂vriga best√§mmelser i detta avtal.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p148 ft5">in this Article means payments of Prop. 2013/14:149 any kind received as a</P>
<P class="p149 ft3">consideration for the use of, or the right to use, any copyright of literary, artistic or scientific work including cinematograph films and films or tapes for radio or television broadcasting, any patent, trade mark, design or model, plan, secret formula or process, or for information concerning industrial, commercial or scientific experience.</P>
<P class="p150 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The provisions of paragraph 1 shall not apply if the beneficial owner of the royalties, being a resident of a Contracting State, carries on business in the other Contracting State in which the royalties arise through a permanent establishment situated therein and the right or property in respect of which the royalties are paid is effectively connected with such permanent establishment. In such case the provisions of Article 7 shall apply.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p68 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Where, by reason of a special relationship between the payer and the beneficial owner or between both of them and some other person, the amount of the royalties, having regard to the use, right or information for which they are paid, exceeds the amount which would have been agreed upon by the payer and the beneficial owner in the absence of such relationship, the provisions of this Article shall apply only to the </SPAN><NOBR>last-mentioned</NOBR> amount. In such case, the excess part of the payments shall remain taxable according to the laws of each Contracting State, due regard being had to the other provisions of this Convention.</P>
<P class="p151 ft3">19</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>

<P class="p93 ft3">Prop. 2013/14:149 4. F√∂retag i en avtalsslutande stat, vars kapital helt eller delvis √§gs eller kontrolleras, direkt eller indirekt, av en eller flera personer med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten, ska inte i den f√∂rstn√§mnda staten bli f√∂rem√•l f√∂r beskattning eller d√§rmed sammanh√§ngande krav som √§r av annat slag eller mer tyngande √§n den beskattning och d√§rmed sammanh√§ngande krav som annat liknande f√∂retag i den f√∂rstn√§mnda staten √§r eller kan bli underkastat.</P>
<P class="p168 ft5">5. Utan hinder av best√§mmelserna i artikel 2 till√§mpas best√§mmelserna i denna artikel p√• skatter av varje slag och beskaffenhet.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p33 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">Enterprises of a Contracting State, the capital of which is wholly or partly owned or controlled, directly or indirectly, by one or more residents of the other Contracting State, shall not be subjected in the </SPAN><NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State to any taxation or any requirement connected therewith which is other or more burdensome than the taxation and connected requirements to which other similar enterprises of the <NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State are or may be subjected.</P>
<P class="p169 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The provisions of this Article shall, notwithstanding the provisions of Article 2, apply to taxes of every kind and description.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p12 ft11">Article 24</P>
<P class="p37 ft4">Mutual agreement procedure</P>
<P class="p171 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">Where a person considers that the actions of one or both of the Contracting States result or will result for him in taxation not in accordance with the provisions of this Convention, he may, irrespective of the remedies provided by the domestic law of those States, present his case to the competent authority of the Contracting State of which he is a resident or, if his case comes under paragraph 1 of Article 23, to that of the Contracting State of which he is a national. The case must be presented within three years from the first notification of the action resulting in taxation not in accordance with the provisions of the Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p172 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The competent authority shall endeavour, if the objection appears to it to be justified and if it is not itself able to arrive at a satisfactory solution, to resolve the case by</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_31">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p32 ft3">√∂msesidig √∂verenskommelse med den beh√∂riga myndigheten i den andra avtalsslutande staten i syfte att undvika beskattning som strider mot avtalet. √ñverenskommelse som tr√§ffats genomf√∂rs utan hinder av tidsgr√§nser i de avtalsslutande staternas interna lagstiftning.</P>
<P class="p173 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">De beh√∂riga myndigheterna i de avtalsslutande staterna ska genom √∂msesidig √∂verenskommelse s√∂ka avg√∂ra sv√•righeter eller tvivelsm√•l som uppkommer i fr√•ga om tolkningen eller till√§mpningen av avtalet. De kan √§ven √∂verl√§gga i syfte att undanr√∂ja dubbelbeskattning i fall som inte omfattas av detta avtal.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p106 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft23">De beh√∂riga myndigheterna i de avtalsslutande staterna kan tr√§da</SPAN></P>
<P class="p32 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">i</SPAN><SPAN class="ft31">direkt f√∂rbindelse med varandra i syfte att tr√§ffa √∂verenskommelse i de fall som angivits i f√∂reg√•ende punkter.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p12 ft5">mutual agreement with the Prop. 2013/14:149 competent authority of the other</P>
<P class="p107 ft3">Contracting State, with a view to the avoidance of taxation which is not in accordance with the Convention. Any agreement reached shall be implemented notwithstanding any time limits in the domestic law of the Contracting States.</P>
<P class="p174 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">The competent authorities of the Contracting States shall endeavour to resolve by mutual agreement any difficulties or doubts arising as to the interpretation or application of the Convention. They may also consult together for the elimination of double taxation in cases not provided for in the Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p175 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft23">The competent authorities of the Contracting States may communicate with each other directly for the purpose of reaching an agreement in the sense of the preceding paragraphs.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p12 ft11">Artikel 25</P>
<P class="p62 ft4">Utbyte av upplysningar</P>
<P class="p176 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">De beh√∂riga myndigheterna i de avtalsslutande staterna ska utbyta s√•dana upplysningar som kan antas vara relevanta vid till√§mpningen av best√§mmelserna i detta avtal eller f√∂r administration eller verkst√§llighet av intern lagstiftning i fr√•ga om skatter av varje slag och beskaffenhet som tas ut f√∂r de avtalsslutande staterna eller f√∂r deras politiska underavdelningar eller lokala myndigheter, om beskattningen enligt denna lagstiftning inte strider mot avtalet. <P class="p177 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft36">Upplysningar som en avtalsslutande stat tagit emot enligt punkt 1 ska behandlas som hemliga p√•</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p12 ft11">Article 25</P>
<P class="p62 ft4">Exchange of information</P>
<P class="p67 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">The competent authorities of the Contracting States shall exchange such information as is foreseeably relevant for carrying out the provisions of this Convention or to the administration or enforcement of the domestic laws concerning taxes of every kind and description imposed on behalf of the Contracting States, or of their political subdivisions or local authorities, insofar as the taxation thereunder is not contrary to the Convention. The exchange of information is not restricted by Articles 1 and 2.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p93 ft5">Prop. 2013/14:149 som medger undantag fr√•n eller neds√§ttning av skatt inte till√§mpas p√• inkomst som s√•dant bolag f√∂rv√§rvar och inte heller p√• utdelning som betalas av s√•dant bolag.</P>

<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p33 ft3">Best√§mmelserna i detta avtal ber√∂r inte de privilegier vid beskattningen som enligt folkr√§ttens allm√§nna regler eller best√§mmelser i s√§rskilda √∂verenskommelser tillkommer medlemmar av diplomatisk beskickning och konsulat.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p33 ft3">Nothing in this Convention shall affect the fiscal privileges of members of diplomatic missions or consular posts under the general rules of international law or under the provisions of special agreements.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4">
<DIV id="id_4_1">
<P class="p127 ft11">Artikel 28</P>
<P class="p181 ft4">Ikrafttr√§dande</P>
<P class="p131 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">De avtalsslutande staterna ska skriftligen p√• diplomatisk v√§g underr√§tta varandra n√§r de √•tg√§rder vidtagits som enligt respektive stats lagstiftning kr√§vs f√∂r att detta avtal ska tr√§da i kraft.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p182 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft38">Avtalet tr√§der i kraft den trettionde dagen efter det att den sista av dessa underr√§ttelser tagits emot och ska d√§refter till√§mpas</SPAN></P>
<P class="p183 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft38">i fr√•ga om k√§llskatter, p√• belopp som betalas eller tillgodof√∂rs den 1 januari det √•r som f√∂ljer n√§rmast efter den dag d√• avtalet tr√§der i kraft eller senare,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p184 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft23">i fr√•ga om andra skatter p√• inkomst, och skatter p√• f√∂rm√∂genhet, p√• skatt som p√•f√∂rs f√∂r</SPAN></P>
<P class="p185 ft5">beskattnings√•r som b√∂rjar den 1 januari det √•r som f√∂ljer n√§rmast efter den dag d√• avtalet tr√§der i kraft eller senare.</P>
<P class="p186 ft3">34</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4_2">
<P class="p12 ft11">Article 28</P>
<P class="p37 ft4">Entry into force</P>
<P class="p187 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">Each of the Contracting States shall notify in written form the other through diplomatic channels of the completion of the procedures required by its law for the entry into force of this Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p188 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft17">The Convention shall enter into force on the thirtieth day after the receipt of the later of these notifications and shall thereupon have effect</SPAN></P>
<P class="p188 ft3">a) in respect of taxes withheld at source, for amounts paid or credited on or after the first day of January of the year next following the date on which the Convention enters into force;</P>
<P class="p189 ft3">b) in respect of other taxes on income, and taxes on capital, on taxes chargeable for any tax year beginning on or after the first day of January of the year next following the date on which the Convention enters into force.</P>
</DIV>

<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p33 ft3">Vid tillf√§llet f√∂r undertecknandet av avtalet mellan Sveriges regering och Georgiens regering f√∂r undvikande av dubbelbeskattning och f√∂rhindrande av skatteflykt betr√§ffande skatter p√• inkomst och p√• f√∂rm√∂genhet, har de avtalsslutande staterna kommit √∂verens om att f√∂ljande best√§mmelse ska utg√∂ra en integrerande del av avtalet:</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p33 ft3">At the moment of signing the Convention between the Government of Sweden and the Government of Georgia for the avoidance of double taxation and the prevention of fiscal evasion with respect to taxes on income and on capital, the Contracting States have agreed that the following provisions shall form an integral part of the Convention:</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t21">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td195"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Med h√§nvisning till avtalet:</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td151"><SPAN class="p39 ft3">With</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td9"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">reference</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td121"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">to</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td111"><SPAN class="p3 ft18">the</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td195"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td196"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Convention:</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td121"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td111"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4">
<DIV id="id_4_1">
<P class="p192 ft5">S√•vitt avser Georgien ska med uttrycket ‚Äùpolitiska underavdelningar och lokala myndigheter‚Äù f√∂rst√•s <NOBR>‚Äùadministrative-territorial</NOBR> units‚Äù och ‚Äùlocal self governing authorities‚Äù.</P>
<P class="p193 ft5">Till bekr√§ftelse h√§rav har undertecknade, d√§rtill vederb√∂rligen bemyndigade, undertecknat detta protokoll.</P>
<P class="p194 ft5">Som skedde i Tbilisi den 6 november 2013, i tv√• exemplar p√• svenska, georgiska och engelska spr√•ken, vilka √§ger lika vitsord. I h√§ndelse av skiljaktigheter ska den engelska texten ha f√∂retr√§de.</P>
<P class="p195 ft3">F√∂r Sveriges regering</P>
<P class="p196 ft3">Diana Janse</P>
<P class="p197 ft3">F√∂r Georgiens regering</P>
<P class="p62 ft3">Nodar Khaduri</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4_2">
<P class="p198 ft3">In the case of Georgia, the term ‚Äúpolitical subdivisions or local authorities‚Äù means ‚Äúadministrativeterritorial units‚Äù or ‚Äúlocal self governing authorities‚Äù.</P>
<P class="p199 ft5">In witness whereof the undersigned being duly authorised thereto have signed this Protocol.</P>
<P class="p200 ft3">Done at Tbilisi this 6<SPAN class="ft39">th </SPAN>day of November 2013, in two copies, in the Swedish, Georgian and English languages, each text being equally authentic. In case of any divergence, the English text shall prevail.</P>
<P class="p37 ft3">For the Government of Sweden</P>
<P class="p201 ft3">Diana Janse</P>
<P class="p62 ft3">For the Government of Georgia</P>
<P class="p62 ft3">Nodar Khaduri</P>

<P class="p202 ft3">F√∂rhandlingar med Georgien om ett skatteavtal genomf√∂rdes i Stockholm i januari 2012. Vid f√∂rhandlingarna paraferades ett utkast till avtal med tillh√∂rande protokoll. <P class="p205 ft4">Lagr√•det</P>
